## Subject: Fw: Criciúama 1
From: Joseph Andrews <jakaal@myldsmail.net>
Date: Wed, 03 Jun 2009 04:20:00 GMT

[jakaalhide_hotmail.com]--Forwarded Message Attachment--Subject: Criciúama 1From: jakaal@myldsmail.netTo: mp8-dansie@ldsmail.netDate: Mon, 27 Aug 2007 21:01:05 +0000Elder AndrewsElder GilóCriciúma 1Zone TuberãoDear President Dansie,        This week was well.  We had two baptisms who were wonderfull.  I remembered that you had said it was likely that Elder Giló would be transferred, so I have prepared to be able to show a new person around but more especially, I have been paying attention to the way he treats investigators and members alike, and I have most observed that the thing which makes him effective is his love for them which so shown in his every action and conversation.  While we teaching an investigator about prayer and scripture study this week I remembered something that president Cardon told us to be effective; Get close to the Savior and stay there.  It occurred to me that the way we do this is to pray in the name of the Savior every day and feast on the words of christ every day as well.  The council of the prophets is always the same: pray, read the scriptures and keep the commandments.  The things that qualify us for ''the work'' are Faith, Hope, Charity and Love with and eye single to the Glory of God.  These are the things that help us to ''know thee and Jesus Christ whom Thou hast sent''.  These are the things that lead us to Eternal Life.  It takes Faith in Jesus Christ to pray in His name and fulfill the At-one-ment of us to God through being one with the Savior to speak to the Father.  All other attributes are stems from our knowing of the Savior and Father, this helps us to change our desires and become more like him.  I love the Gospel of Jesus Christ and how real it is the more you ponder upon it.       Elder Giló is Amazing.  Thank you for letting us be companions in my first transfer.  I am sad he is leaving, but we all have things to do in our times.  I just remember hte parable in section 88 in the doctrine and covenants.  tudo bem.       Our area is excellent, the members love us and I love to sing to them at almoso and strengthen them.  We have a family that isn´t golden, but platinum.  they want ot be baptized before they go to spain in ttree weeks so we have to work fast.  We also have a group of friends who are doing well if we can get them to come to church on their own.        The things that came to me when we were teaching I taught in a bit easier way to understand and I think the investigators took it well.  I feel that if they can pray to their Father in Heaven they will recieve their own testimony.  they may say that they prayed, but I want tehm to Truly pray.Our numbers this week;2212/5121960115290/10

My companion and I get along very well, and I find that I learn more and more from his methods of teaching and how well he sets up his commitments and challenges.  I love and look up to him.      Our work moves on, we work hard and find and teach many people.  we have several progressing investigators and some new investigators which have great potential as their hearts are open.  the members are friendly and love us very much.       This week went well despite the rain and other less than favorable weather.  It seems that each time it rains, we find someone that is waiting for us.  This was the case on Thursday, friday and saturday.  Particularly on saturday when we found a family that was perfect and the mother had searched for the truth and was still ready to recieve the truth.  Her son said that he was going to spain in a couple of weeks and asked if we had a church their and if so he would get baptized there if he had to.  It was remarkable because we were trying to find there house(it was a referral for the gospel blesses families booklet) and it was dark and raining, but we kept going.  It was just like President Faust said about the extra mile hours that we keep going and get the rewarding moments of life.Our number this week:0016/5411350/3174140/15          God Bless and thank you for the work you do for us. [jakaalhide_hotmail.com]--Forwarded Message Attachment--Subject: Elder Andrews CriciúmaFrom: jakaal@myldsmail.netTo: lamontedansie@gmail.comDate: Mon, 23 Jul 2007 20:27:01 +0000Elder Joseph Levi AndrewsElder Gilóarea Criciúma 1Tubarão zoneDear Presidente Dansie,       All in all I have enjoyed my first week in the field.  My companion is very supportive and helping.  It seems that the main qualification of a trainer is to be able to teach lessons in full with a little input from someone that has a hard time speaking.  I love to teach however and even though I can´t speak but a few sentences on many subjects, when I teach with desire to convey the importance of a special subject or priciple, the spirit takes over.  I am very grateful to bea able to teach not with words, but with the spirit.  I love the Lord and enjoy doing his work.       I love Elder Giló as he is a hard worker and very supportive.  We get along well, we work hard and he always knows what we are doing.  We pray together and bear testimony to each other.  It is good to be with one so positive.       I really like the members here, they are very generous and willing to assist us and the people of Criciúma are wonderful.  It amazes me how open about they are about their feelings.  We have a few investigators that are doing well, and I hope we are able to solve their concerns as they come up when we teach the commandments.  Brasil is Beautiful.       My first night here we shared a brief message about the plan of salvation with the boyfriend of a sister we are teaching.  He interrupted to say that he was having feelings concerning our way of teaching that he never had had and wanted us to come over on sunday to eat italian food and teach him more.  Two other investigators shared their testimonies with us about the truth of the book of mormon and the church without us asking and they are both marked for baptism.  I love the opportunity to serve the Lord through serving his children and wish to do the best I can.thank you for everything you do for us and God bless. ## Subject: Fw: hello from criciúma!
From: Joseph Andrews <jakaal@myldsmail.net>
Date: Wed, 03 Jun 2009 04:22:00 GMT

[jakaalhide_hotmail.com]--Forwarded Message Attachment--Subject: hello from criciúma!From: jakaal@myldsmail.netTo: skipandrews@sprintmail.netDate: Mon, 23 Jul 2007 19:50:32 +0000dear family,        sounds busy back at home!  And that was a huge email that dad sent.  I really had a good time recalling the things that dad does to keep the van running.  i remember the time when he took off the engine cover and had a paint dip stick in some part or other and when the van wouldnt work right, he would jiggle it.  one time it spit fire back at him.  Or the time when we drove to the east coast on something like 4 cylinders...       I´m glad that the family adventures went well.  i´m not particularly impressed with the flying in brasil, as we waited on the runway for an hour in São Paulo and a couple of hours later a plane flew off the runway.  Its kind of strange to think that that could have been me.  all in all i´m glad to have gotten to Floripa safely.  it´s beautiful here.  São Paulo was extremely feio (ugly) because Every thing is concrete.      We were all right in supposing that the CTM is mini america.  In Criciúma we don´t have hot water or washing machines so shaving and washing the dishes are less than favorable experiences in the mornings when its roughly forty degrees.  But I really like it here.  we have a ward and the Irmãs-sisters feed us ALOT.  if i eat three plates of beans and rice, they think i don´t like their food.  I eat lunch with them and i don´t eat dinner and i´m not hungry when I go to bed.  my new companion Elder Giló is cool, he has a great sense of humor and is very supportive of my português.  Its really hard to teach, but the the spirit takes over and covers up my very limited português.       I didn´t know that dad was writing a book!  Thats really cool.  I hope the new Harry Potter book is good.  I find i don´t care much for the attitudes of the main characters in the recent books.  there are alot of hills here and my legs burn alot so hopefully I won´t gain weight from all the arroz e fejão.         sounds like aurelia is tearing up the town in Olathe.  Boys, music, -all she needs now are some guys in huge basketball jerseys on the street corner selling mountain dew and a bentley and she could rule the city.  just kidding.  which quintett is she playing? Dvorák?  sounds cool.  well my time is expired so take care and know that I love you.  tell Grandma thatnk you for teh email, I was just studying section 138 a few weeks ago and dispelled some false docrtine that someone told me.  it´s a marvelous chapter with the book of moses.              Love Elder Andrews

I really like the members here, they are very generous and willing to assist us and the people of Criciúma are wonderful.  It amazes me how open about they are about their feelings.  We have a few investigators that are doing well, and I hope we are able to solve their concerns as they come up when we teach the commandments.  Brasil is Beautiful.       My first night here we shared a brief message about the plan of salvation with the boyfriend of a sister we are teaching.  He interrupted to say that he was having feelings concerning our way of teaching that he never had had and wanted us to come over on sunday to eat italian food and teach him more.  Two other investigators shared their testimonies with us about the truth of the book of mormon and the church without us asking and they are both marked for baptism.  I love the opportunity to serve the Lord through serving his children and wish to do the best I can.thank you for everything you do for us and God bless.           Elder AndrewsOur Numbersbaaptism/confirm                       0/0data de batismo                          7/3pesquisadores na sacremental      3lições com membro present         7outras lições                               14recebidas/contatados                  0/3novos                                         18menos ativos                              5contatos e endereços                  125/20

In Criciúma we don´t have hot water or washing machines so shaving and washing the dishes are less than favorable experiences in the mornings when its roughly forty degrees.  But I really like it here.  we have a ward and the Irmãs-sisters feed us ALOT.  if i eat three plates of beans and rice, they think i don´t like their food.  I eat lunch with them and i don´t eat dinner and i´m not hungry when I go to bed.  my new companion Elder Giló is cool, he has a great sense of humor and is very supportive of my português. I hope the new Harry Potter book is good.  I find i don´t care much for the attitudes of the main characters in the recent books.  there are alot of hills here and my legs burn alot so hopefully I won´t gain weight from all the arroz e fejão.         sounds like aurelia is tearing up the town in Olathe.  Boys, music, -all she needs now are some guys in huge basketball jerseys on the street corner selling mountain dew and a bentley and she could rule the city.  just kidding.  which quintett is she playing? Dvorák?  sounds cool.  well my time is expired so take care and know that I love you.  tell Grandma thatnk you for teh email, I was just studying section 138 a few weeks ago and dispelled some false docrtine that someone told me.  it´s a marvelous chapter with the book of moses. I have sadly discovered that the Brasileiros don't realy specialize in or take delight in cookies, ice cream, sweets or any other manner of deliciousness which is fot the joy of mankind.  they do have paçoca though, which is like powdered peanut butter.  its more or less scrumptuously-delightful.      Ive made a few discoveries in the book of mormon these past few weeks.  I once had a home teaching companion tell me that we couldn´t repent or change after this life because of what it says in alma's letter to corianton in alma 46ish and it made me mad.  we are still people and to say  that we cannot change demeaned and denied the power of the atonement so i studied.  result- we can change and repent in the spirit world, and after the ressurrecion, we are made to permanantly as we are at the time of the resurrection.       Also, as i was reading in alma 32 i read verse 40 and asked the question: do we plant our own tree of life through our heed to the word?  I had always supposed that the seed spoken of was faith, but on colser analysis, it says the word is the seed.  furthermore, in the folowing chapters when amulek speaks, he makes reference to the word bein in christ which references John 1:1-15.  some food for study if any one wants to take the time.      well i love you all and hope to hear from you next week                Love,                        Elder andrews

So I talked to him in a general way and taght him about the attitude we should have as missionaries based on D&amp;C 5:4- namely charity, and everything turned out fine.  I firmly believe their are two basic facets to obedience.  first, obedience to the commandments, which my companion, and most of the district does well, and more importantly, to obey the governing principles of the law.  if you can obey the principles, you can discern when it is appropriate to use the spirit of the law as opposed to the letter of the law.  whenever you follow the spirit of the law, you go to a higher point in the law, NEVER to break the law.  unfortunatley, most people don`t recognize this and i think this is the reason we have a in-finite number of law in the US to specify when it counts or not.           any way, i´d rather have an uber obedient companion than an undermotivated and disobedient companion.  Contrary to popular belief i do have to do my own laundry. I know that the Power of the ressurection is real, that we can gain a forgivness of our sins through the atoning sacrifice of Jesus Christ and that as we gain faith in him, we will see the sun, the fowers adn the trees, and we will see the light of the TRUTH:  All these things exist for the express purpose of our attaining the bithright of GODhood, for this is the work and the  glory of GODs; to bring to pass the maturity of their children.
